Local News 188

Jiao Tong University

Preparation for the Industrial and Railway Exhibition is Nearly Completed

To Be Held for Ten Days Starting on the 30th of This Month. 207 Chinese and Foreign Exhibitors. Over 100 Experts to Attend the Conference.

Individuals Wishing to Visit Can Request Admission Tickets by Mail.

The National Jiao Tong University has scheduled to hold an Industrial and Railway Exhibition for ten days starting on the 30th of this month. The details have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Now, with the exhibition date approaching, the preparatory work is extremely intense. The collection of exhibits and the layout of the venue are mostly nearing completion. The latest news is recorded below in detail:

Chinese and Foreign Exhibits 189

Various companies, factories, institutions, schools, and railway administrations, both Chinese and foreign, have been successively transporting exhibits. As of yesterday, there were 54 Chinese factories and companies, 11 railway administrations including Longhai, Beining, Jinpu, Pinghan, Jinghu, Xiang'e, etc., 12 local and foreign institutions, 7 schools, 10 American factories, 30 British factories, 27 German factories, 7 Swiss factories, 4 Italian factories, 26 Belgian factories, 5 French factories, 3 Canadian factories, and 1 each from Russia, Sweden, Hungary, Denmark, and the Netherlands. Combining other aspects, there are a total of 207 exhibitors. In terms of engineering exhibits, electrical machinery is the largest category, followed by photos, charts, and models. In terms of railway exhibits, in addition to products from the 11 Chinese railways such as Jinpu, European and American railway material companies also have a large number of valuable exhibits. All kinds of engineering machinery will be started at the time to allow visitors to understand the living organization of the machines and stimulate their interest in observation.

A Glimpse of the Layout 190

The layout of the venue has now been revised and finalized as follows: The industrial exhibition is located in the Engineering Hall, the railway and municipal exhibition is located in the Upper Courtyard, the road association's road and municipal exhibition is located in the South Dormitory, the heavy engineering machinery exhibition is located in the shed factory, the achievement exhibition of Tangshan and Shanghai colleges is located in the gymnasium, and other events such as the opening ceremony, expert conferences, Mandarin speech contests, amusement parties, music concerts, university meetings, and dinners are located in the Engineering Hall, Ronghong Hall, gymnasium, Wenzhi Hall, etc. A large archway has been built at the entrance of the venue, with a large sound amplifier installed by the China Wireless Electric Research Society. Its sound can be heard by tens of thousands of people. On both sides of the pedestrian paths inside the venue are suspended the school's circular school emblems, with the national flag inserted on top and yellow tassels hanging below, each school emblem is also equipped with a red lamp, each being over one foot long. The perimeter of the large playground is decorated with red-edged electric lights, with a large lighthouse in the middle, rotating all day and shining light at any time. The top of the Engineering Hall is equipped with a large loudspeaker by the American Asia Company, and a large searchlight is set up by the British Tongming Electric Company. Various decorative lights are hung at the entrances of each hall. The entire venue is laid with a light rail by the National Economic Commission, and its locomotives and vehicles are supplied by the Chanson Foreign Company. All exhibitors have specially requested local art advertising companies to decorate the venue, so the decorations are very luxurious and beautiful. A part of the layout has already been completed, and the other part is actively being arranged and will be completed soon.

Expert Conference 191

In order to gather domestic celebrities to exchange opinions, the school previously sent letters to various relevant institutions, schools, and industrial and railway experts across the country, inviting them to hold an expert conference during the exhibition period to discuss major issues such as industry, railway, education, and national defense, so that they could use this opportunity to discuss common goals and jointly plan appropriate progress. It is now learned that this conference has been scheduled to be held on the mornings of April 1st, 2nd, and 3rd. Currently, more than 100 people have responded, including Wei Tingsheng, Ma Yinchu, Yu Chengzhi, Gao Luming, and Wang Erzhen. More than a dozen papers have also been received, which are currently being compiled for exchange during the conference. As for expert lectures, it is planned to invite Shao Lizi, Zhou Fohai, Fu Kaisen, Yu Youren, Jiang Zuobin, Ma Xiangbo, and a dozen other people, and invitation letters have already been sent.

Achievement Exhibition 192

The school's Achievement Collection Group held a special meeting last week, chaired by Qiu Weiyu and recorded by Yang Yaowen, to discuss the following key issues: 1. How should the collection of the school's achievements be carried out separately? It was resolved to request each department, faculty, office, and library to collect self-made achievements, as well as products from student groups or individual faculty and staff members. 2. How should the classification of achievements be determined? It was resolved to classify them as follows: (A) Historical evolution of the school; (B) Photos, brochures, and publications on the equipment status of each department and faculty; (C) Personal writings; (D) Personal manufactured products; (E) Student academic achievements (such as reports, plans, charts, papers, monographs, publications, notes, exercises, test papers, experimental results, factory products, etc.); (F) Sports achievements; (G) School-made products and self-made instruments. 3. Should models and specimens be displayed? It was resolved to display them selectively. 4. Should factories and laboratories be open to visitors? It was resolved that each department head should plan and arrange the factories and laboratories that can be demonstrated themselves. 5. How should the exhibition locations be determined? It was resolved that they should be displayed in the gymnasium, the communication room, and the billiards room. 6. How should the exhibition rooms be arranged? It was resolved that (A) charts and photos should be hung on the walls; (B) academic achievements bound into volumes should be classified and displayed on examination tables; (C) various or each type of achievement should be marked separately to make them eye-catching. 7. How should the marking format be determined? It was resolved to ask Yang Yaowen to plan. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Amusement Park 193

The school has scheduled a national music performance on the evening of March 30th, a Beijing opera performance on the evening of April 1st, a music concert on the evening of April 2nd, an amusement park on the evening of April 4th, and a drama performance on the evening of April 7th. Every day, the Navy, the Public Security Bureau, the Yutong School, the Orphanage, and the school will take turns performing military music. Educational films of industrial products from famous factories in various countries will be shown every night. Yesterday, Dean Zhong of the Management College, the director of the group's preparation, told a reporter from the Shanghai Social News that in this time of serious national crisis, it is not appropriate to be extravagant, but in order to arouse the interest of the audience, we have to add some amusement to help the fun. As for the various amusement performances, it is planned to sell tickets uniformly, with ticket prices divided into two types: 2 dimes and 5 dimes. All ticket income will be used to purchase aircraft, etc. As for the admission tickets to the exhibition, no fees will be charged. They will be distributed to various schools and institutions. Individuals who wish to visit can request them by sending a formal letter.

March 27th at the Old Site of the County Education Bureau

Essays

### Movie Propaganda 214

— Zhan Lu

Movie propaganda that encourages the spirit of the people and promotes national glory is more genuine and profound than any other kind of propaganda. Since the September 18th Incident, the film industry in our country has made considerable contributions to anti-Japanese war photography; however, it cannot compare with the strong and great influence of films with themes of love, romance, fantasy, and chivalry.

While the Japanese militarists created the history of aggression since the September 18th Incident, they used all their strength to promote war films that encouraged the people. In particular, the "Three Human Bullets" they touted were three soldiers under the command of Company Commander Kawano Junji during the January 28th Battle of Miaohang: 1. Ekaishita, 2. Kitagawa Jo, 3. Sakae I之助, who all sacrificed themselves by carrying bombs and charging into our army's positions. They believed that having these "Three Human Bullets" was a glorious event in their war history. The number of films produced by various film companies about these "Three Human Bullets" was: Shinto Company, 41 films; Gansai Company, 28 films; Fukui Company, 26 films; Akazawa Company, 22 films; Kawai Company, 20 films; Dainichi Company, 11 films; Yoshikawa Company, 7 films; Shochiku Kamata Company, 6 films, totaling 161 films. This shows their fervent admiration for the "Three Human Bullets."

Recently, General Song's victory at Xifengkou was also a glorious page in our war history. The number of warriors willing to act as human bullets far surpassed their mere "Three Human Bullets." After 500 members of the Broadsword Brigade hacked to death over a thousand Japanese soldiers defending the city, only 20-odd survived. Such heroic sacrifices are worth all the people in China's film industry making films about all 400-plus martyrs. They made over a hundred films about their "Three Human Bullets"; we have 400-plus human bullets, so even making thousands of films would not be too many. In order to encourage the people and promote national glory, we must devote ourselves to movie propaganda as much as possible.

Furthermore, the enemy will commend the names of the "Three Human Bullets"; will we just let the 400-plus human bullets be nameless heroes? I believe it is necessary to commend the names of all the national heroes who made heroic sacrifices.

### Records of Flowers in Suzhou 215

— Zheng Yimei

Plum blossoms bloom first in spring and are worthy of appreciation for their unique fragrance. The Fragrant Snow Sea of ​​Dengwei is particularly famous. Everywhere, high and low, there are calyxes and green flowers. Shi Deyuan's poem says: "Halfway up the mountain, human smoke is in the fragrant snow, and chickens and dogs are in the white clouds below." This shows how beautiful the environment is. However, in recent years, mountain people have found planting plum trees to be less profitable, so they have planted mulberry trees instead, interspersed with magnolias. When the flowers bloom in spring, tourists come from all directions to buy boats and wear wax clogs, but they inevitably feel a sense of prosperity and decline compared to the past. The plum blossoms at Piyun Nunnery at the foot of Lingyan Mountain and Lengxiang Pavilion in Tiger Hill are all beautiful, with the charm of rain bathing the fat and rouge, and smoke covering the jade. The botanical garden in the city is now a nursery, and it is also a place to view plum blossoms. The iron-bone red plum blossoms in Keyuan, with branches and leaves of ocher color, are particularly unique.

Peide Hall is located in Bailianjing. The peonies are very lush and are known as the "Fragrant Kingdom of Flowers." Ladies and gentlemen travel there in an endless stream. After Grain Rain, they are all pruned. Therefore, there is a saying that peonies are pruned three days after Grain Rain.

The Master of the Nets Garden in Kuojiatou Lane is privately owned. Its Dianchun 　 is where 　peonies and herbs are planted.

Huanxiu Villa is located in front of Shen Yamen. The last blossoms bloom, monopolizing the elegance.

Panchi Mountain, commonly known as Nanshan, is located southwest of Danshan. There are many peach trees on the shady side of the mountain. In spring, it looks like a brocade curtain.

The Eight Banners Guild Hall has wisteria planted by Wen Zhengming. It twists and turns like a dragon, occupying several acres of land. When it blooms, it is colorful and dazzling, like hanging jewels. Looking at it always makes people miss the elegant virtue and pure style of Mr. Hengshan.

The Qingyang Causeway is lined with cherry blossoms, all white like snow. It is the location of the Japanese Consulate. Since the Japanese pirates invaded and feelings have worsened, no one goes there to enjoy the flowers anymore.

The lotus flowers in Huangtiandang outside Fengmen are lush and green, stretching for several miles. The flowers stand out proudly from the leaves, like Xiangfei emerging from the water. Tourists often hire boats before dawn. The dewdrops are still running on the plates, not yet dry. Suiyuan in the city has twin lotuses. The Qixiang Guild Hall in Wen Yali, east of Baolin Temple, has many lotuses in its pond, which come from the Seven Ze of Xiaoxiang. The exotic species are precious.

The Conggui Villa of Huiyin Garden is surrounded by osmanthus trees, all of which are three or four fathoms high. The millet-jade sticks to the branches, as if storing ten thousand loads of fragrance.

The Xiangzhou of Zhuozheng Garden has poems about camellias by Wu Meicun engraved on its screen. Only the precious pearl flower with thousands of layers clustered together is a pity that it has withered. It is said that there are plans to replant it. If so, then under the bamboo and beside the plum trees, delicate figures will play in the shadows, and the cold season will not be lonely.

### Big Belly 216

— Fang Xin

There is a Chinese proverb that says: "A prime minister can moor a boat in his belly." A good (boat-mooring) belly is a very big one. But this is not the case. The proverb simply means that the prime minister has a big capacity.

Recently, while reading Mr. Wu Yifeng's "Deng Chuang Cong Lu," there was a passage that said: "An Lushan's belly hung down past his knees and weighed 352 catties. See Yao Runeng's 'An Lushan's Deeds' and Qian Xiyi's 'Southern New Book.'"

This (weighing 350 catties) is probably not the weight of the (belly). There will never be such a heavy (belly) in the world. But this (belly) that can (hang down past the knees) can also be said to be a very big belly.

### Fire 217

— Zhang Ningyi

Humans have these two (eight) eyes, so (fire) came into being.

Because A Mao had two eyes, he saw his wife in love with someone else, so he was filled with anger and went to catch the adulterer. A Gou took a fancy to someone else's young lady, so he did something like rape. The other party got angry and sued in court. These are all initiatives of fire (meaning anger), and they added a lot of news to the newspaper out of thin air.

But before the fire, there was a disaster! At the end of the Ming Dynasty, Wu Sangui, in a fit of anger, planted a seed for the Manchu puppet state that exists now, more than 200 years later. Wu Sangui borrowed Qing troops for Chen Yuanyuan, and the Manchus took this opportunity to enter the Central Plains and passed it down to Puyi. The Republic of China was established and the empire was overthrown. This Emperor Xuantong lived in seclusion in Beiping. Who knew that now the dwarves wanted to expand their territory, so they picked Puyi, this treasure, to be a puppet ruler, resulting in the so-called Manchuria. Just imagine Wu Sangui's anger at that time actually affected China 200 years later!

However, fire is ultimately great. Burning Yibi is still a beautiful story to this day, and it also aroused Mr. Dongpo's interest in a night tour of Yibi in the Song Dynasty.

However, people are always extremely terrified of it, but they dare not stay away from it. Even the biggest figures have to go hungry if they don't have it. But if you get too close to it, it will immediately burn up all your property and turn it into a flat ground!

Here, I think of this fire (anger) that is burning fiercely in the Three Islands recently. The general public, for the sake of the unfounded Wanbaoshan case, were filled with anger and invaded our Northeast, established a puppet state, and further occupied Rehe. But looking back at our country; it is truly worthy of being a cultural ancient country of thousands of years. It is ridiculous that the young deputy commander has no fire at all? No matter how barbaric the Japanese are, they can't ignite his fire! As for the dying old undead Tang Yulin, there is no need to mention it. Originally, cooked soup without fire would not be able to maintain and become cold soup, right? If fire had a soul, it would only sigh at these two.

### The North Station of the Future 218

— Cheng Zhizheng

Since the January 28th Incident, the North Station has been burned down by Japanese aircraft bombing. After the end of the war, the Ministry of Railways wanted to build a joint transportation station in Zhenru, and planned to sell the land of the current North Station to fund the construction of the new station. The scale of the joint transportation station would naturally be exceptionally magnificent and grand, taking approximately two years. And because the joint transportation station could not meet the urgent need, a temporary station was specially built on Song Park Road to serve as an application. The plan was decided, the foundation of the temporary station was being laid, the land in Pengpu Township was also demarcated, and everything was being prepared.

Now, because the war in the north is very serious, the Ministry of Railways has decided to temporarily postpone the original proposal to move the station. The Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau, based on the Ministry's order, is now starting to restore the old station. This plan is to rebuild the destroyed building. The design is as follows: the entire building is divided into two floors, the lower floor is the same size as the original site, and the upper floor occupies approximately one-half. There is also a mezzanine in the two floors, which is not visible from the outside.

This building is entirely allocated to the Traffic Department for use, and the remaining departments have all moved to the Riverside Building at the intersection of North Henan Road. The Traffic Department's arrangement is to set up the Commercial Documents Section on the ground floor and mezzanine, and the Dispatching Section and Reading Room on the second floor. After the new station is built, there will also be bars, public telephone booths, and commercial counters on the ground floor, all adopting commercialization to correct the bad habits of the past bureaucratic style.

The new station can be completed in about three months. From then on, the destroyed old site will be covered with a beautiful and magnificent building again.

Long Novel

### Northeast Fourth Company Commander 219

— Zhang Henshui

Zhao Weng said again: "It's not that I'm saying something presumptuous, but the demise of the Great Qing Dynasty was due to this point. The officials of the Qing Dynasty ate and drank, and didn't care about anything like enriching the country and strengthening the army, or planning for the people. They just talked about empty slogans. If two acquaintances greeted each other on the street, they would ask about each other, from big to small, and it would take at least three or four minutes to ask about everything. One person asked a greeting, and the other person would answer with a greeting as usual. Even if you didn't ask, you knew that's how they would answer. Isn't this a bunch of nonsense? Why bother? So I feel that in this day and age, it doesn't matter if young people's manners are a little sloppy, as long as they are busy doing things all day long like you two, then they are the number one good people. Big girl, don't be so reserved, eat!" Saying that, he grabbed a handful of melon seeds and stuffed them into Guizhi's hand. Old Wang had already come in and poured tea again. Guizhi pinched the melon seeds, squatted slightly and thanked him. Zhao Weng repeatedly shook his head and said: "I've said it before, we don't need to be polite." Guizhi smiled and said: "Although that's what you say, I can't be so informal to my elders." Zhao Weng said to Jiang Shi: "What did I say? This girl of yours is reasonable, and can be both rough and refined. My Ziqiang is considered a good kid, and doesn't have any of the habits of a soldier. He earns enough money to support me. But he has official duties, and father and son can't always be together. Although he is now stationed in Xiyuan, as long as the superiors give an order, saying 'let's go,' maybe he'll be transferred today. How can I, as a father, follow him? So I manage the accounts for others in the shop, and I don't want to come back. It's not for anything else. In other people's shops, there are shopkeepers and partners who are always together, so I just muddle along like this and it's not lonely at all. If I didn't do it, what's the point of an old man living at home? Now, I reluctantly let the child pick me up, and just live with such a servant. If I had a girl like your big girl by my side, I would be much happier." Jiang Shi smiled and said: "We only moved in two days ago, and the old master has said these words several times. Otherwise, let's aim a little high and have this child kowtow to you and become your goddaughter."

Whereabouts

### Liwa Chestnut Village Girl 220

— Chonglou

Di came to my house to see me, and I arranged with her to spend a clear and sunny Sunday afternoon in the Liwa Chestnut Village in Western Shanghai.

When the car finally flew over the Zhongshan Road Bridge and sent us to the pier of Liwa Chestnut Village, the bustling city had already left us far behind! We waved at the pier; the old woman on the opposite side shook the boat over to ferry us to the other shore.

We walked through the lane, and a clear river appeared in front of us. On the other side of the river was a green lawn, and yellow thatched huts were planted in the corners of the field. A few children in red clothes looked like fruits in the field from a distance. We walked along the river and sat down on a stone step by the river.

"Listen! The sound of birds in the branches, the barking of dogs outside the village, our eardrums haven't been in contact with these natural sounds for a long time!" My mind seems to be liberated, I said to Di like this.

"Look! The clear stream in front of us, why can't it wash away the accumulated dirt in our hearts?" Di stared intently at the leisurely flowing water. The sun shone on the smooth water surface, reflecting a dazzling golden yellow.

A warm and soft breeze blew over us, and I sang softly: "Wind: Be careful when you blow, don't blow the flowers down..." I looked at Di's hair again, which had already been messed up by Aunt Feng, so I told her a story about "wind blowing scattered hair."

"The sound of oars, the fate of mountains and rivers!" Although this place lacks verdant mountains, the green water is enough for us to be intoxicated. Our boat has been paddling forward, and the riverside grass seems to be proudly saying to the duckweed in the water: "I am not like you, when I see a boat coming, I have to make way."

When we were tired of traveling and went back, the village was playing farewell music, and the setting sun showed the report for the evening. Finally, Di played on the swing at the head of the village for the last time, which ended a pleasant spring outing of half a day.

### Daocheng Mountain 221

— Xizong

The season is telling us that it is already spring. ? Spring is in the countryside, and it wants to give people intoxication and temptation. So I packed up my selling body, dragged my tired body, and after a day's journey, the succession of trains and ships, I finally arrived in my hometown, ran into the countryside, and went to ask about spring.

A group of us partners set off to Daocheng Mountain, passing by the tomb of Chen Yingshi along the way to make a moment's mourning. There were no incense candles and paper ingots, no wine, rice and flower circles; only a goose-yellow tender willow with budding branches in my hand, and a passion burning in my chest. I paid my silent respects.

We walked many uneven stone roads, and under the guidance of our partners, we ran into a farmer's house and stayed for a moment. In the middle of this farmer's house, five photos were hung in the center: Cai Tingkai, Jiang Guangnai, Dai Ji, Zhang Zhizhong, and Chen Mingshu, heroes of our nation, have deeply penetrated the people. Undoubtedly, it has gained the respect of the public.

When the corner of the red wall was exposed in the mountainside, we knew we were almost there; but because of the earth's gravity, we couldn't get there for a long time. Isn't that what's in front of us? The four characters of the Fuhu Zen Temple have been spread out in front of us. Running to the mountain gate, the first thing we saw was Master Fuhu. According to legend, there was a fierce tiger here that was conquered by him, so a temple was built for him. That's the history of this place. We ran to the top of the mountain again, standing under the tower: looking at the small Huzhou, and the winding highway. And this intoxicating spring breeze has tempted my entire soul. Although we came to ask about spring, except for a few spring breezes, everything was still in the embrace of winter.

When we ran out of the mountain gate, the herdsboy had already ridden on the back of the cow, and bursts of bell sounds came from the temple. Monk, do you know? (Being a monk for a day and ringing the bell for a day is still an empty game.)

Free Talk

### On Article Formulas 222

— Yu Kuifu

China's national affairs, such as politics, military affairs, finance, and diplomacy, are never on track and run wild like mustangs. Only one thing, articles, is always regular and orderly, and has been the same for thousands of years. Xie An of the Jin Dynasty commented on Zhang Hua's articles, saying: "Even if Duke Zhang wrote thousands of articles, they would still be the same." This sentence can still be applied now. Novels with triangular or pentagonal love affairs need not be mentioned. Even military telegrams always begin with "Heavenly disasters and civil wars have risen in China," in the middle they always use "If Qingfu is not killed, the disaster in Lu will not end" to denounce, at the end they always use "I will not offend others unless I am offended" as an oath, and finally they always use "Old comrades-in-arms, talented people in the sea" as witnesses. And the changes in wording are especially minimal. However, the articles on social events in the newspapers are such that there are these articles every day, in every issue, but the authors never get tired of them, and the readers don't seem to find them annoying. Let me first copy a formula: "So-and-so from so-and-so place, in the prime of her youth, a modest maiden 丨or approaching puberty, graceful or still charming in her old age丨, and Mr. So-and-so, fell in love at first sight, and formed an inextricable bond, starting with secret rendezvous, followed by open courtship 丨or one night stand丨, and then she became pregnant, with a big belly, recently they are as affectionate as a couple, living together as if husband and wife."

These few sentences cannot be missing from any social news report, as if they are chicken soup or MSG in a dish. As for the plagiarism of predecessors in poetry and the verbatim copying in essays, it can be forgiven if it is skillfully prepared. But in a social news report of only a few hundred words, this set of elaborate drumming is always repeated. I really don't understand the psychology that makes both the author and the reader feel interested.

### One Aspect of Saving the Country Through Aviation 223

— Zhang Tianyi

As long as you are a Chinese, you naturally know the importance of aviation. Saving the country through aviation should be participated in by everyone. Therefore, whether female, male, old, young, poor, or rich, they are all practicing donating money to buy airplanes.

At the same time, airplane tours are also being implemented.

So some people spend 50 silver dollars just to sit on an airplane for fifteen minutes for a tour.

This cannot be compared to those small clerks, elementary school students, and workers who save a few cents from their living expenses to make aviation donations.

But it is said that: at this time of bright spring, it is possible to take a trip in the air to broaden your mind and body. This is very good for your health. Good health can avoid the ridicule of being the sick man of East Asia, and it is also a way to win glory for the country.

Moreover, before, there was a woman who used her own natural feet to serve the country in front of the foreign devils. Later, during the national crisis, there were celebrities who fasted to save the country with their stomachs, and at the same time, there were those who used their conscience, using a good heart to save the country. In that case, things on a person's body can be used to save the country. Therefore, it is necessary to broaden your mind and body, broaden

It's good, so as to save the country. It is also necessary.

Therefore, the effect of spending 50 silver dollars is equal to an aviation donation. This kind of aerial tour is also one aspect of saving the country through aviation.

### Liar 224

— Shi Heng

In ancient mythology, there was a story written like this: a woodcutter lost his axe, which was his only property. Losing it was the same as losing the way to live, so he knelt in the mountains and shouted to the sky, hoping that God would give him another axe. How miserable was this shouting! But I heard a similar miserable shout in the modern urban society.

One spring, near dusk, after a day of work, I went out of my room to prepare to go to the park. Just as I was about to cross the wide street, I saw a crowd of people gathered on the pedestrian path on the opposite side of the street. I went over to see, and in the crowd surrounding it, there was a slanting, overturned carrying pole, with many broken dishes scattered around. The owner of this carrying pole was an old man, wearing extremely tattered shorts and jacket. His legs, as thin as dry firewood, were completely exposed. His face was pale and terribly thin, and only a few sparse white hairs topped his head. His frail and pitiful body, carrying a carrying pole on the bustling streets of such a city, was bound to fall down at some point. But that carrying pole, the dishes on that pole, and the pot containing something like a powdered dumpling were his entire life, all his property. If the dishes and broken pot were broken, he would no longer be able to carry that pole to the street the next day, and then there would be no place to find rice for his life the next day.

He was picking up the broken dishes from the ground, crying loudly and jumping, which was exactly the miserable situation of the woodcutter in the modern city who lost his axe and shouted to the sky.

The people surrounding him were all sympathizing with him, but no one gave alms. At that time, I touched my pocket, and there happened to be a silver dollar inside. I stretched out the hand holding the silver dollar from the crowd, and the poor old man immediately knelt in front of me. I hurriedly turned and walked away.

Walking in the park, I thought about this. At dinner, I talked to my wife about this. Late at night, lying in bed, I was still thinking about this, and whenever I thought about it, my mood immediately became depressed.

My unhappiness seemed to be because this modern city showed its sin, but for this matter, I only saw half of it, and I did not fully understand it: I only saw half of the sin of this city, and I did not fully understand it.

Later, not long after, on another street, I saw another crowd of people gathered. In the crowd, there was the exact same scene as described above, and I recognized that still crying and jumping frail old man at a glance. I stared at the crowd surrounding it, the broken bowls and pots, and the crying and jumping old man, and a new discovery immediately appeared in my mind, and I said unconsciously: "Ah, this is a kind of deception!" This time no one gave alms, no matter how pitiful the old man's cry was. Soon, the police on the road came, dispersed the crowd, and ordered the poor old man to quickly pack up and leave. The old man wailed even louder, the police got angry and wanted to arrest him, and the old man simply rolled on the ground and refused to get up. I didn't have the patience to finish watching this scene, and I immediately walked away.

Walking on the road, this matter tormented my heart. At this time, my unhappiness was even more than before. At first I thought that this was a kind of deception. Later I thought that the old man who could not survive without resorting to such a miserable deception was even more pitiful. This city, this evil Shanghai, this devil's den that forces a frail old man to perform this kind of deception, should be destroyed soon. In the end, I regretted, why didn't I take out a little more money to help that poor old man before the police arrived!

The Crossroads of Era and Love 225

— Zhang Guanping

"Hai Quan" Mo Mingqi Miao asked back in confusion.

"I want to write a eulogy couplet and send it to your home for you to hang up." ("I dare not, I dare not.")

Hai Quan said "I dare not" twice, ignoring Mr. Zhu and hurriedly jumped out of the car.

Twenty-Seven

Hai Quan finally found the alley where Cao Shiguang lived, near the Chinese streets of the concession. He thought, "This is the residence of the semi-poor and struggling." He saw that at least one chamber pot was placed at the back door of each house, and Hai Quan felt a little disgusted when he saw it. He found the house number and called at the front door for a while, but there was no response, so he went to the kitchen door at the back. The back door was open, and Hai Quan boldly stepped in. "Who are you looking for?"

A short, stout middle-aged woman with bound feet blocked his way.

("Is there a Mr. Cao, from Guangdong, living here?")

("There is.")

The woman seemed very arrogant, and it took a while before she replied loudly, "There is." If Hai Quan hadn't been a bit more tolerant this morning because of his fight with the Japanese, he would have argued with this local second landlord based on his usual temper.

("Is he at home?")

Hai Quan endured his anger and asked again.

("Who knows? Why don't you go up and see for yourself?")

The woman with bound feet ignored him and walked towards the front hall. Hai Quan thought, "Why are the Chinese always so unfriendly? They don't even want to help people with things that don't require any effort. They are always unhappy and impatient when telling people they don't know which way to go. Do they still want to live in this world? The philosophy of 'everyone sweeps the snow from their own doorstep and doesn't care about the frost on others' roofs' is too developed in China. No wonder the Chinese in the north are fighting with the Japanese, while the Chinese in the south are happily drinking with Japanese diplomats."

Hai Quan went straight up to the second floor alone. The attic and front rooms on the second floor were all locked. Therefore, there was no light on the staircase in between. He groped for a while before he could vaguely make out the dim outline of the staircase area. He went to the door of the front room and knocked.

("Who is it?")

A singing-like female voice. He thought, "This is undoubtedly Mrs. Cao. I met Mrs. Cao once at the church that day."

("It's me. Is Cao Shiguang at home?")

("Who are you?")

Again, a singing-like tone. Hai Quan imagined that Mrs. Cao was asking his child, which was why she was making such a moving, melodic sound.

Odds and Ends from Paris 226

— Xiao Shijun from Paris

(6) The World-Shaking Natural Feet

Natural feet are naturally bare feet. But here, it also carries another meaning, referring to the feet of celestial maidens. Because the magic of celestial maidens' feet is truly powerful. Regardless of whether they are natural feet, as long as they belong to a celestial maiden, they can make people kneel before them. The "lotus flowers with every step" praised by ancient Eastern poets and scholars were not natural feet. But they often faithfully confessed to willingly bowing down to pomegranate skirts, and Westerners are the same. Although they worship natural feet, aren't the owners of these two feet all celestial maidens? Regardless of ancient or modern times, regardless of China or abroad, foot worship is probably human nature. If scientists encounter this, they can simply define it as a general rule.

However, when I went to the Moulin Rouge in Paris to see Mistinguett's dance, I couldn't help but feel a surprising sense of astonishment. She is a world-renowned dancer who has accumulated millions of gold solely with her two feet. Not only has she captivated thousands upon thousands of Parisians, but also the serious-looking British and Germans, the culturally sophisticated Italians, the Spaniards who produced the mad knight, the Americans who want to pave the entire earth with gold, and even the Jews, sons of God who want to redeem humanity, are all followers of her two feet. I thought to myself, "Since her two feet have such great power, she must be a celestial maiden who can save sentient beings with her beauty." But when I saw her dancing naked on the stage, I felt not so much the joy of being drunk with gold and paper, but rather a heartbreaking sorrow. Life! Life! A fleeting life like lightning and flint! It disappears in an instant! Mistinguett, the owner of the world-shaking natural feet, although she used 100,000 gold as insurance for one of her feet, and adding the other, it is naturally 200,000, this number can greatly shock the poor Easterners, but she can never use gold to retain her youth. She is now over sixty years old. She has amazing skills. When she dances, I feel that the transformation of Guanyin, as described by the poet Wu Meicun of my country, "bending her back and sticking to the ground, the lotus flower spitting," is not enough to describe even a ten-thousandth of it. However, ruthless time cannot forgive her after all, and countless lines are engraved on her jade face day by day. Perhaps because I am an amateur when it comes to dancing, when I watch her perform, I feel that it is not as interesting as watching a plump young girl in another entertainment hall, Folie Bergere, rise and fall on the stage, like thousands of reds and purples waving in the spring breeze. To me. Their elastic waists, the interweaving of straight lines and curves, and the soul-stirring rhythm, in the eyes of connoisseurs, compared with Mistinguett, naturally have a distinction between elegance and vulgarity, but I think it is not so far apart.

Sure enough, I am not alone in this regard. Since Paul Morand wrote an article titled Magie Noire to promote black art, Parisians have developed a special interest in the dances of primitive peoples in the Near East. And these dancers are mostly in their prime. When they stand naked in the center of the stage, like bronze statues, there is a simple and pure fragrance that penetrates the heart. A certain black woman was even praised by Parisians as the Black Venus. And the Indian dancer Nyota Inyoka also became famous for a while. Her dances are divided into four types: ancient Indian dance, modern Indian dance, ancient Egyptian dance, and modern Egyptian dance. She has never been to India. She was originally born from a mixture of Indian and Egyptian people. Her dance costumes and stage equipment all come from her personal designs, so they have a different flavor. Later, a pure Indian girl, Shan Kar, also achieved considerable success on the stage performing pure Indian dance. Other dances of various shapes and colors, one after another, all compete with Mistinguett, the owner of the world-shaking natural feet, for a day's glory. Therefore, now her fame is gradually like her age, with a feeling of the sun setting in the west.

Bond Stagnation Intensifies

Yesterday, the trend in the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange and public bonds remained sluggish. There seemed to be a gradual emergence of bulls on the No. 47 bond, but the volume of retail investors entering the market was not strong, leading to a noticeable decrease in trading. Most were still in a holding pattern, observing the situation. With no definite progress in diplomatic and military matters, the market was dull, and bond trading appeared slow and weak. In the morning's first session, several of the leading bonds rose slightly by one or two cents. However, later, due to some selling of the No. 47 bond, they fell back by one or two cents, and investor sentiment seemed slightly weakened. In the second session, there was even more selling of the No. 47 bond. Although there was some demand for the No. 1 and No. 11 bonds, supply still exceeded demand, leading to a drop of two or three cents, sometimes even four cents or more. The afternoon session opened with still sparse investor interest, and market prices were unusually stable, with highs and lows differing by only one or two cents. The distant salt tax bonds were particularly firm. At the close, demand for the No. 11 bond was relatively high, and retail investors were also buying in, pushing the price up uniformly by one to four cents, with the consolidated salt tax being particularly strong. As a result, apart from the April issue of the 1929 bonds, which rose slightly by five points, the remaining bonds fell slightly by one to five cents or more. Regarding the March futures, as the settlement date approaches, the bulls and bears cannot maintain this stalemate for long, and a fierce competition is expected within the next two to three days. Yarn Exchange Announces Change to National Currency Pricing 236

The local Yarn and Cloth Exchange has already resolved that cotton yarn transactions will be priced in silver dollars starting with the September term, and cotton transactions will be priced in silver dollars starting with the October term. The unit of cotton will be five silver cents, and the unit of cotton yarn will be ten silver cents. Also, for cotton yarn transactions starting with the September term, each piece should pay a basic margin of eight yuan in silver dollars, and those who should pay an additional margin should pay four yuan in silver dollars per piece. For cotton transactions starting with the October term, each picul should pay a basic margin of three yuan in silver dollars, and those who should pay an additional margin should pay one yuan and five jiao in silver dollars per picul. Also, considering that September is the time when cotton is between seasons, trading in the September term should be suspended for one month starting from April.

Downriver Rice Drops in Price After Peak

Flour and Wheat Both Deserted 238

Flour: After the market opened in the morning, prices for each month generally showed a calm trend. Prices for imported wheat, both US and Canadian, were down by about ten to twenty cents, so the market sentiment was flat after the opening. Both buyers and sellers tended to shun each other, and development was difficult. Ultimately, due to the increasingly severe situation in the north and the extremely tight silver supply for various road merchants, there was no interest, which was a natural trend. By the time the afternoon session opened, the market for each month tended to be flat and weak again. Henan merchants slightly sold out this month, while smaller factories engaged in hedging. For the distant months, larger factories continued to sell, but because there were limited buyers, the number of sales was few. Currently, imported wheat is still arriving continuously, so the factories' selling has not stopped. As a result, this month was down slightly by two and a half cents from the previous day, the April, July, and August months were slightly better by two and a half cents, and the May and June months were unchanged.

Wheat: After the market opened in the morning and afternoon, prices for each month tended to hover and stall. Imported wheat was down by ten to twenty cents, and buying and selling in all directions was unusually desolate. Merchants who had no relationship with it did not even inquire, so although imported wheat had significant ups and downs, the market hovered as usual. It can be seen that the lifelessness of the market is not something that can be remedied in a short period of time. As a result, the prices for this month to August were the same as the previous week.

Oil Market 241

White Tung Oil Weak Development

Since the foreign trade of white tung oil has been decreasing year by year, the market has almost become a slump. Recalling the prosperous atmosphere of the past, one cannot help but feel the rise and fall. Although the producing areas of Sichuan and Hunan have suffered losses, they have expressed their willingness to hold on to not sell cheap. However, with no hope of a turnaround, holding on for a long time only increases costs, and even if there is a loss, they have to sell it painfully. As such, the market cannot be saved. According to the details of the Hankou letter, 800 to 900 piculs of Xiang tung oil were opened for sale, priced at eleven taels and seven cents in cash, and 150 piculs of Hunan support basket tung oil, at eleven taels and seven cents, including tax. Foreign firms have not traded for several days, and the price is still around fourteen taels and six to eight cents. Hankou firms wholesale at around eleven taels and six to seven cents. The local tung oil firms believe that the price of Hankou tung oil is similar to that of Zhejiang tung oil, so the goods can be sold both south and north. Last night, Hangzhou firms came to Shanghai to sell 200 to 300 pieces, priced at 22 yuan and six jiao, for foreign sales, but the market was extremely sporadic, so there were no large-scale transactions.

Key to the Safety of the European Situation 249

France Prepares to Join

European Four-Power Pact

British and French Prime Ministers Meet Today

Germany's Attitude Still Unexpressed

Reuters, London, 20th: According to the latest news from Paris today, the talks between the British and Italian prime ministers in Rome have indeed shown signs of improving the European situation. According to Paris news, there is now a possibility of rapprochement between France and Italy. It is heard that after consulting with cabinet members tonight, French Prime Minister Daladier and Foreign Minister Bonnet will tell the British counterparts at the meeting tomorrow that the French government is willing to support the work of the British authorities in Rome. It is believed that the repeated statements in recent days of the talks on how much good results can be achieved in the diplomacy of European countries without the use of force will certainly have a very pleasant psychological effect, so as to promote the restoration of world trust. According to informed sources, France is preparing to participate in a convention of mutual consultation, but at the same time, France must have sufficient time to study the details.

France Studies in Detail 250

Havas, Paris, 20th: This agency's diplomatic correspondent believes that when French Prime Minister Daladier and Foreign Minister Bonnet meet with British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon tomorrow, they will express friendly support for the plan proposed by Rome. The French authorities believe that the Italian plan is a diplomatic expression that will have a significant impact on the development of international relations in European countries. Moreover, because the French have always had objectives that are in line with the Italian plan, the French authorities are particularly willing to support the Italian authorities' peaceful policies. As for the measures to prohibit the use of force, it will certainly have a very good psychological effect at present, and it will be of great benefit to restoring world credit. Therefore, France is prepared to participate in the proposed treaty. However, at first glance, there seem to be some points in its implementation that need to be substantially amended. French representatives will have to request a long-term study. The world should know that this treaty will include the revision of peace treaties and the recognition of Germany's equality of armaments, and its impact will be far-reaching. Therefore, France must first study it in detail and understand its reasons before it can sign it.

The United States Also Attaches Great Importance 251

Havas, Washington, 20th: The plan proposed by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has attracted great attention from political and journalistic circles, but the State Department remains silent. The State Department is deeply aware of the difficulties in bringing the views of France and Germany closer together, and regards the Italian plan as a way to restore peace in Europe. President Roosevelt believes that the recovery of American industry and commerce depends on the success of the disarmament conference and the world economic conference, and even partial success will be beneficial. Therefore, Roosevelt is very worried about the overall situation in Europe. American disarmament representative Davis will probably meet with French Foreign Minister Bonnet.

Havas, Rome, 20th: The local press is very happy about the results of the talks between the British and Italian prime ministers, but their arguments are very prudent. The Italian newspaper Il Popolo d'Italia said that the policy of combining the four major powers is not a new name today, and its purpose is to start uniting from the main members of Europe, so as to achieve peace in Europe. The newspaper Il Messaggero said that the Italian plan is only to restore order between countries, and does not target any country. The organ newspaper Il Lavoro Fascista said that British Prime Minister MacDonald fully agreed with Mussolini's views.

Havas, London, 20th: Political circles have criticized the results of the talks between the British and Italian prime ministers, and are quite in favor of the newspaper's explanation of yesterday's communiqué, saying that it can reconcile the interests of those who agree to amend the treaty and those who agree to maintain the status quo. However, the Manchester Guardian raised a point that it considered to be very important. The newspaper believes that amending the treaty may harm Poland.

Small Entente Worries 252

Havas, Belgrade, 20th - Political figures here are quite worried about the proposed Four-Power Committee plan by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, which excludes the Balkan Small Entente nations (i.e., Yugoslavia, Romania, and Czechoslovakia), and believe that this policy may bankrupt various organs of the League of Nations.

Havas, Washington, 20th - The plan proposed by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is not only applicable to the four major powers, it is explained here, saying that it can prove the importance of tomorrow's talks in Paris between British and French authorities. Also, because MacDonald is very concerned about Poland and the Small Entente countries, the key to the problem lies in the meeting in Paris.

Havas, London, 20th - The Cabinet met for half an hour this afternoon to discuss foreign policy, with particular emphasis on negotiations in Geneva and Rome.

Roosevelt Assassination Case 253

The Murderer Goes to His Execution Calmly

Heavy Guard Around the Prison

Reuters, Lealford, 20th - Zangara, the murderer who failed to assassinate President Roosevelt and mistakenly killed the mayor of Chicago, went to his execution calmly in his prison cell at 9:15 this morning. Dressed in striped cloth pants, a white short shirt, socks but no shoes, he went straight to the electric chair, looked back at the jailer and said, "You know, I am not afraid of death, don't bother to catch me and seat me." After speaking, his expression remained unchanged, he sat down boldly, and listened to the jailer placing the leather straps on his hands and feet, and adding an iron cap to his head. After the arrangement was completed, there were about thirty people in the room. Zangara asked, "Are there any people here who have brought a camera to film me?" The jailer replied, "No." Zangara then shouted, "Capitalists are a bunch of cunning thieves!" Then he leaned back in his chair, smiled and said, "I bid farewell to the world, goodbye." In an instant, the electric button was turned, his body straightened, his head stretched out, and his hands remained in their original position. After three minutes, the current stopped, and this strong murderer had already died. Before his execution, Zangara gave a roll of paper to the prison official, saying that it was a manuscript of his book. This morning, the prison was heavily guarded, with two machine guns placed on the roof to prevent accidents. At 9:27, the authorities announced that Zangara was dead, but how to dispose of his body has not yet been decided.

Japanese Opposition 256

MacDonald Disarmament Convention

Naval Ministry Instructions to Be Mailed to the Japanese Delegation in Geneva

Saying That Its Content Is Based on Europe and Has Nothing to Do with the Far East

Dentsu, Tokyo, 21st - British Prime Minister MacDonald's disarmament plan will be put on the agenda of the General Committee of the Disarmament Conference on the 25th. The Japanese delegation in Geneva telegraphed the Naval Ministry yesterday, requesting that the research materials necessary for discussion be sent to Geneva. The Naval Ministry plans to mail them this month. The Japanese government will express its full opposition to the British plan. The opinions of the naval authorities are summarized as follows: 1. The British plan consists of five parts, namely, security guarantees, arms reduction, concessions and exchanges, scientific warfare, and the Standing Disarmament Committee. It only aims to concretize the decisions made by the Disarmament Preparatory Committee. The figures, in addition to adopting the Hoover plan and the British claims, only add security guarantees, scientific warfare, and the establishment of a Standing Disarmament Committee, and have no fresh significance whatsoever. Its content is entirely based on Europe and has nothing to do with the Orient. 2. Regarding the six articles on security guarantees in each part, it is intended to negate the conclusions that are effective against countries that violate the non-war treaty, and its content is abstract and has no concrete plan. It is expected that France will express its opposition and the agreement cannot be established. The second section of the second part on disarmament, and Articles 25 to 33 of the second chapter, cannot be supported by Japan for the following reasons: (A) The London Naval Treaty is a provisional treaty until 1936. It will be revised after 1937, but this plan does not change it and prolongs it, so it cannot be supported. (B) It is absolutely opposed to establishing this as a universal general treaty with countries around the world. (C) From a practical point of view, according to this plan, an agreement can be reached at the earliest at the end of the year. When the Five-Power Naval Conference in 1935 is imminent, the effective period of this agreement is only one year. Therefore, there is no need to rush to conclude this agreement today. It is more effective to establish regulations on naval armaments other than those of the London Treaty countries. (D) At the Geneva Disarmament Conference, since a new agreement with different content has not been established, this plan has not once given the Japanese disarmament plan that should be submitted at the 1935 Naval Disarmament Conference a formal opportunity for proposal, so full vigilance must be maintained. (E) In Chapter 3, regarding the abolition of aerial bombardment in Article 34, the Japanese side reserves its support because it is related to the total abolition of aircraft carriers and other matters. (F) In Article 37 of Chapter 3, the military weight of aircraft shall not exceed 3,000 tons. This is to remove the threat from European countries. For Japan, a country with the longest coastline, it is most necessary to prepare aircraft with continued power, which is different from the situation in Europe. (G) Article 41 of Chapter 3 restricts the aircraft of the six countries of Britain, Japan, the United States, France, Italy, and Russia to 500 aircraft, and wants to establish an abolition regulation. It cannot be agreed to unless an agreement on land and sea forces and the absolute prohibition of aerial bombardment is established.

Soviet Defense in the Five-Year Plan 275

This article is a report by Voroshilov, Chairman of the Military Committee of the Soviet People's Committee, at a meeting of all party workers in the Moscow garrison on January 20, 1933, translated from the Izvestia newspaper on January 24, 1933.

The growth and development of the Soviet Red Army are progressing simultaneously with the growth of the proletarian state, not lagging behind the development level of its productivity and technology. In fact, it cannot but be so, because the Soviet Union is now in the midst of an imperialist hostile encirclement. Without perfect and sound military equipment, it cannot exist for a day. Therefore, the Soviet government pays special attention to the Red Army. At the same time, Soviet national defense cannot but be reflected in the five-year plan.

Since its history, the Red Army has proven that it has fulfilled its duties to the fullest extent. We have repeatedly declared to the workers, peasants, and masses across the country that in order to fulfill its duties, the Red Army will never allow the enemy to cross the sacred border of the Soviet Union under any circumstances. This oath is indeed true. The strength of the Red Army lies in its special political and moral status and spirit, as well as its high degree of revolutionary consciousness.

The Red Army's arms were inherited from the old Tsarist Russian army, and the old Tsarist Russian army was the most backward in Europe. During the revolutionary period, the improvement of the Red Army's weapons relied only on the military equipment seized from the White Guards and foreign imperialist intervention forces during combat. In the years after the end of the civil war, during the recovery period, the Red Army's weapons were still not improved, firstly because the Soviet Union did not yet have an industrial foundation sufficient to solve this major problem, and secondly because the old army did not leave behind skilled military cadres. All the military equipment of the old army was imitated or imported from foreign countries. Therefore, it is the basic task of the five-year plan in national defense to seek technical transformation of the Red Army based on the progress of the new industrial industry. Therefore, reorganizing the Red Army based on the establishment of a new type of weapons manufacturing industry is also the focus of our work.

During the five-year plan period, the results in this regard are no less than in other aspects. The Red Army at the end of the five-year plan is very different from the Red Army in 1927 and 1928, just as the current economic structure of the entire Soviet Union is different from that in 1928.

To what extent has the technical transformation of the Red Army now reached?

First of all, in terms of machine gun weapons, the significance of machine guns in modern defense is known to the world. In short, modern army lower-level organizations, even down to small units, cannot defend themselves without sufficient machine guns of various types. At the end of the World War and thereafter, in defensive battles (such as defending against infantry, aircraft, and tank attacks), in addition to heavy machine guns, there were also portable machine guns, anti-aircraft machine guns, and large-caliber machine guns, etc. For this reason, in 1928, the Soviet Red Army had nothing but heavy machine guns, namely the old Maxim machine guns. Even the heavy machine guns were relatively few in number. At that time, the Red Army had no portable machine guns at all. What it had were various old-fashioned machine guns made abroad. These machine guns were not only technically too old, but also extremely scattered and insufficient for military use. Therefore, they were also military equipment with very little combat power. What was especially fearful was that at that time, there was no foundation for manufacturing heavy artillery at all.

In addition, at the time of the Soviet Union's prosperity, it naturally had no aircraft machine guns, no anti-aircraft machine guns, and no tank machine guns. Therefore, in the five-year plan, our efforts to reorganize military equipment focused first on the supply of new and powerful machine gun weapons of various types.

Significant achievements have indeed been made in this area. The Soviet Union can now manufacture all the above-mentioned machine guns, and their styles are no less than the latest in foreign countries. Especially in the manufacture and invention of rifles and machine guns, a large number of military equipment technicians, experts, gunsmiths, and young engineers have been trained and are still continuing to study and improve. These talents are all selected from workers in old machinery factories and have now become reliable and experienced military technology cadres. Their technical knowledge is keeping pace with the rapidly advancing technology of Europe and the United States. It is no exaggeration to say that the technical problems facing the Red Army can be solved easily. The Soviet Union has now invented new automatic rifles, automatic pistols, and other new types of military equipment. These military equipment are being manufactured on a large scale in Soviet factories.

During the years of the five-year plan, the Soviet Union not only created new shooting and machine gun weapons, but also established a new military industry. If the enemy attacks the Soviet Union, the Red Army will have sufficient automatic weapons to guarantee.

The Red Army's artillery weapons were even worse before. The significance of artillery combat equipment in modern warfare is extremely important. After the World War, the armies of capitalist countries made rapid progress in improving artillery and artillery systems. The old artillery of the armies of France, Britain, Italy, and the United States has been almost entirely modernized. In terms of range and speed, they have reached the point where nothing can be added. Not only that, but also the relationship between artillery units has fundamentally changed, and the number of shell guns used has greatly increased, and many new types of military equipment have been added.

In this area, the Soviet Red Army's difficulties are no less than in shooting and machine gun weapons. In the manufacture of shooting and machine gun weapons, it is still possible to select the required talents from the old gunsmiths, but in the manufacture of artillery weapons, there is no design at all. What the old army left behind is either dead, uneducated, or affiliated with the pro-Soviet regime. So we retrained talents and established a design agency dedicated to very complex and technically advanced work. Now the Soviet Union's old artillery has also been renovated, and the achievements made in range and speed are no less than those of the new artillery in Europe today. Whether it is small-caliber guns or various new heavy artillery and new anti-aircraft artillery, the Soviet Union can manufacture them itself. The lower-level organizations of the Red Army, even platoons and companies, are equipped with all kinds of artillery to resist tanks, all kinds of special military equipment carried by infantry platoons and companies, and weapons to defend against enemy short-range machine gun nests.

In addition, we have also invented many new types of artillery. The results of the tests have been very good. They are now being manufactured on a large scale in Soviet factories.

What is the main victory in this area? It lies in the fact that during the first five-year plan, the Soviet Union established a strong foundation for manufacturing its own artillery, established a powerful ordnance design bureau, trained skilled talents and engineers for military equipment manufacturing, and established many factories sufficient to solve the problems of the Red Army's artillery equipment. (To be continued)

The Father of a Japanese Woman 276

Kneels Down to Sell His Daughter into Prostitution

(Havas Tokyo Correspondence) It is often the case that young Japanese women are sold to brothels by their parents. It is a long-standing custom and is not considered strange. Japanese girls are devoted to filial piety and do not hesitate to sacrifice themselves to use the money from selling themselves to relieve the family's difficulties, which is truly pitiful. But recently, there was an even more peculiar incident, because the person being sold was a married woman, who should obey her husband in principle, and her parents have no right to dispose of her. This woman is twenty-one years old. She married last August and had a harmonious marriage. Last month, her father summoned her to return home, took her to Osaka without telling her the reason. The woman did not think it strange and happily went with him. She did not expect that her father had sold her to a brothel for 800 yen, and she would only be free after five years. The woman was shocked when she heard this and was unwilling to engage in this lowly occupation. Her father knelt down in front of her and told her that the 800 yen had already been paid and was about to be used up, but the family was in difficult circumstances and could not get out of it without this. The woman, unwilling to disobey her father's wishes, tearfully agreed. But then she thought of her innocent husband, how could she bear to betray him? So she escaped from the brothel and went straight to the police station, begging for help. The police also did not know what to do. This is also strange.

European Nations 278

Amounts of War Debts to America

Totaling 11.2 Billion Yuan

According to the Tokyo Jiji Shinpo, after US President Roosevelt takes office, he will actively discuss issues such as arms embargoes, military disarmament, war debts, and Manchuria. First, he will notify the participating advisory committee, followed by addressing the war debt problem. It is found that the total war debt owed to the US by European countries amounts to 11.2 billion yuan. Those with payments due on December 15th of last year included six countries: England, Italy, Finland, Czechoslovakia, Lithuania, and Latvia, totaling 6.5662 billion yuan, specifically: (1) England: 4.398 billion yuan, (2) Italy: 2.0049 billion yuan, (3) Czechoslovakia: 167.071 million yuan, (4) Finland: 8.604 million yuan, (5) Lithuania: 6.198 million yuan, (6) Latvia: 6.885 million yuan. Other countries that did not fulfill payments last December and have suspended negotiations include seven: (1) France: 3.86303 billion yuan, (2) Belgium: 400.68 million yuan, (3) Poland: 206.057 million yuan, (4) Greece: 31.516 million yuan, (5) Austria: 23.752 million yuan, (6) Estonia: 16.466 million yuan, (7) Hungary: 1.909 million yuan. Furthermore, Romania and Yugoslavia are in talks with the US for settlements that are not yet resolved. Their war debt amounts are (1) Romania: 63.861 million yuan, Yugoslavia: 61.625 million yuan. In summary, the total war debt owed to the US by European countries amounts to 11.261178 billion yuan. This month, six countries—England, Italy, Czechoslovakia, Finland, Lithuania, and Latvia—will begin negotiations with the US for 2.765329 billion yuan.

Yang Hucheng 279

Goes to Shijiazhuang to Meet Chiang

Reports on the Recent Political Situation in Shaanxi Province Chiang Greatly Commends Yang’s Measures

Xi'an dispatch: Yang Hucheng led his entourage, including Mi Zanchen and Zhou Fanbo, on an inspection tour of eastern Shaanxi on the 8th of this month. After arriving in Tongguan, he received a telegram from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek summoning him to Shijiazhuang. Yang took the Longhai Railway east on the afternoon of the 8th, arriving in Zhengzhou at 9:30 AM on the 9th. He briefly rested at No. 24 Longhai Road. After breakfast, he headed north from Zhengzhou at 11:00 AM, arriving in Xinxiang at 2:00 PM. Zhang Ji, a member of the Central China Office, and others welcomed him at the station and had a lengthy closed-door meeting in the dining car of Yang's special train. Zhang and others expressed great indignation at the retreat from Rehe without a fight and particularly admired Yang's request to volunteer to fight against Japan. They hoped that Yang could lead troops to the front to carry forward the past revolutionary glory. He headed north at 5:00 PM, arriving in Handan around 11:30 PM. Wang Ziyi, the commander of the 84th Division garrison, greeted him at the station. After a brief conversation, they departed. The train arrived in Shijiazhuang at 5:00 AM on the 10th. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's special train also arrived at the station a quarter of an hour later. Yang greeted him on the platform and then went to Chiang's train for a conversation. He excused himself after about half an hour. At 4:00 PM, he was summoned to Chiang's special train again for an audience. After meeting Chiang, he requested instructions on detailed plans for resisting Japan and reported on the recent political situation in Shaanxi. The conversation lasted about three hours. According to sources, it was exceptionally satisfactory. That evening, Zhang Ji and other Central Committee members from the North China Office came to Shijiazhuang, and Li Zhigang, a member of the Shaanxi Provincial Government, also came from Nanjing. During his audience with Chiang, Yang presented the plan to relocate the arsenal to Luoyang and the second-phase project plan for the Jinghui Canal to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, which were greatly commended. Approval has been granted to submit them to the Economic Committee for review and assistance with funds. On the 11th, Division Commander Jing Yuexiu responded to Yang's telegram and arrived in Shijiazhuang from Taiyuan. They discussed Shaanxi's political and military affairs and disaster relief. Jing and Yang have a deep friendship and have shared hardships for nearly ten years since their separation, so they were very happy to see each other. At 4:00 PM on the afternoon of the 12th, Chiang's special train went to Baoding, and Yang's special train also left Shijiazhuang at 5:20 PM, heading south. At 10:00 AM on the 13th, he arrived in Zhengzhou. He originally planned to return west that afternoon, but according to the Zhengzhou office of the Pacification Commissioner, Chairman Liu of Kaifeng, Director Liu Xueya of Nanyang, and Commander Zhang Boying telegraphed, stating that they were summoned north by Chiang and requested that Yang wait in Zhengzhou. Therefore, he temporarily suspended his departure. That evening, when the trains of Liu, Liu, and Zhang passed through Zhengzhou, Yang greeted them at the station and had a lengthy closed-door meeting. At 4:00 PM on the afternoon of the 14th, the train departed westward, arriving in Luoyang after 8:00 PM. At 8:00 PM on the 15th, he arrived in Tongguan, where he transferred to a car westward. Upon hearing the news, Army Commander Sun Weirou and Army Commander Feng Qinzai went to Lintong to greet him. Chief of Staff Wang and personnel from various departments of the Pacification Commissioner and the heads of various departments of the Provincial Government greeted him outside Zhongshan Gate. Yang finally arrived in the provincial capital at 3:00 PM (on the 15th).

Spring is Mild and the Weather is Warm 280

The Volunteer Army in Northern Manchuria Rises Up

Surrounding Various County Seats and Fiercely Fighting the Japanese Army

According to the Osaka Asahi Shimbun on the 14th, when the Japanese army previously conducted large-scale suppression of the volunteer army in various parts of northern Manchuria, most of the volunteer army was broken up into smaller units or lay dormant in Russian territory, waiting for an opportunity to reorganize. Now that winter has passed and the severe cold in northern Manchuria has subsided, the volunteer army in various parts of northern Manchuria has once again risen up, mobilizing in various places, causing the Japanese army to be exhausted. According to the information received by the Japanese military authorities regarding the volunteer army in northern Manchuria, as follows:

1. On the 8th of this month, the volunteer army attacked the Japanese army stationed in Baoqing County. Both sides engaged in a fierce battle for three hours. Japanese police instructor Ichikawa and Sangji were killed by the volunteer army.

2. On the 10th of this month, the volunteer army leader Sanxia commanded 1,000 volunteer soldiers to occupy Dongning County, capturing and killing Japanese Councilor Kuwahara Ikuo and translator Miura. Two members of the Japanese garrison and two members of the security team were killed, and five Japanese soldiers were injured.

3. At 11:00 PM on the 11th of this month, 400 volunteer soldiers suddenly attacked a small station on the Harbin-Suifenhe line, engaging in a four-hour battle with the Japanese army, killing two Japanese security team members and destroying the railway, causing the train from Harbin to Suifenhe to be temporarily disrupted.

4. On the 11th of this month, Chen Dongshan led 2,000 volunteer soldiers to surround Mishan County. The battle is still ongoing. The whereabouts of Japanese county councilors Yasuda and Fukuda are unknown.

5. On the 13th of this month, Shen Qinglin led a large army to attack Weihe on the Eastern Railway Line and surrounded the county seat, killing Wen Pengshan, the head of the puppet security group.

According to general speculation, a large number of volunteer soldiers will appear in various places along the Sino-Russian border.

Of Antiquities Transported South Arrive in Shanghai

Docking at the Wharf at 3:00 PM Transferring to Automobiles at Jinliyuan

The second batch of antiquities from the Beiping Gugong Museum was transported south to Pukou and then loaded onto the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Kuaili Wheel, totaling two thousand five hundred and fifty-four boxes. Today, the wheel passed the Yangtze River Estuary at 11:00 AM, and the shipowner sent a telegram stating that the wheel, carrying two thousand five hundred and fifty-four boxes of antiquities, was scheduled to enter the Wusong Estuary at 2:00 PM today and dock at the Jinliyuan Wharf in the Nanshi district around 3:00 PM. When the antiquities were about to arrive in Shanghai, Yao Younan of the Beiping Gugong Museum Administration sent a special telegram to the receiving personnel, stating that all loading and unloading of the antiquities upon arrival in Shanghai must be strictly enforced. Yesterday morning at 11:00 AM, President Song sent a special representative to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to negotiate and obtain the procedures for extracting the antiquities. The escorting officer was Yu Guokui. There were also one hundred and fifty military police officers on board to protect them to Shanghai. Regarding the unloading of the antiquities, the Maotai Company will still send a large number of automobiles to transport them to the designated location for storage.

Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center 288

Preparing for the Second Agricultural Exhibition

The Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center is preparing for the second agricultural exhibition to promote farmers' competitive production. The details are as follows:

Notice: China is vast and rich in resources. In recent years, due to the economic aggression of the great powers and the farmers' adherence to old ways, production has been short-lived, and the trade deficit has increased year by year, forming a picture of economic desolation in the countryside. If no measures are taken to encourage production, the consequences will be dire. In order to promote farmers' competitive production, the Center has decided to hold the second agricultural exhibition in April of this year. A preparatory office has been established and letters have been sent to various places to collect products. Shanghai is the central hub for the gathering of special products from China and abroad. We sincerely request that you forward this letter to various industry groups to prepare products and send them for display in order to promote progress and enrich the people's livelihood. We would be extremely grateful.

Methods: (1) The scope of collection is mainly agricultural products from this county. Special products from other counties are also welcome to be displayed at the exhibition. (2) The types of collection include crops, horticulture, forestry, livestock, aquatic products, agricultural manufactures, agricultural implements, films, and circular tables. (3) Collection organizations: district offices, social education organizations, district farmers' associations, and agricultural

organizations. The exhibitors should register and arrange the collected products according to the form, fill in the labels, and send them to the exhibition for display at the specified time. (5) Collection dates: from the 20th of this month until one week before the opening of the exhibition. (6) Disposal of exhibits: Except for the items borrowed for the exhibition, the exhibits collected will be returned or retained as appropriate according to the results of the review. (7) Awards: The exhibits deemed excellent by the evaluation committee will be awarded by the Center.

After inquiring with Guangdong, the Guangdong authorities replied to Shanghai, instructing that the communist bandit be escorted to Guangzhou for investigation and handling.
