A portion of the cabin space was allocated for the military police to reside, so as to provide security along the way.

Yu Mingzhou, Party Committee Member of Heilongjiang Province, Arrives in Shanghai 290

Reports on the Current Situation in Heilongjiang Province and Requests Assistance

Yu Mingzhou, a member of the Heilongjiang Provincial Party Department, was appointed by Chairman Ma as the Commander-in-Chief of the Heilongjiang Provincial Self-Defense Army after the September 18th Incident. He led the Heilongjiang Provincial Militia in a bitter fight against the enemy. Later, due to the exhaustion of ammunition and the lack of reinforcements, he led his troops to retreat into the mountains, waiting for an opportunity to act. Yu himself, along with Dong Shaoliang, the Commander-in-Chief of the First Route of the Northeast Salvation Army, detoured to Beijing. He arrived in Shanghai from Beijing a few days ago to report to all sectors on the current situation in Heilongjiang Province and hopes to provide assistance so that he can take advantage of the enemy's concentration in Rehe and the emptiness in the rear to lead his troops in a counterattack and disrupt the enemy's rear, so as to achieve a pincer attack.

The Great Petition of Marine Engineers 291

Tomorrow to the Maritime Affairs Bureau

Since the Ministry of Communications carefully navigated and strictly formulated the regulations on the qualifications of marine engineers and issued them to the Ministry for verification and issuance of certificates, only those with certificates are allowed to work on commercial wheels. On the one hand, it also instructed the various wheel bureaus to dismiss all marine engineers who do not meet the qualifications, have no academic background, and have not been certified by the Ministry, and to replace them with certified personnel. However, the glorious decree of the Ministry has not been followed by the company, resulting in nearly one hundred marine engineers with certificates being unemployed, while the employment of marine engineers without certificates on the wheels is ubiquitous. Today, all marine engineers who have received the Ministry's certificate have resolved to go to the Maritime Affairs Bureau tomorrow to petition Director Zhu Yaoting, requesting compliance with the Ministry's decree to provide relief and ensure fairness, so as to reduce all kinds of tragedies in the maritime industry.

Accident of Dalian Steamship Company's New Ship 292

The Dalian Steamship Company competed to load Northeast soybeans in order to open the Dalian-Europe route, which was previously reported in this newspaper. The company purchased six 8,000-ton wheels from the Canadian Steamship Company in England with 2 million yuan funded by Mantetsu. The crew and sailors had already been transported to Europe by Nippon Yusen to receive the wheels and sail them back to Dalian. However, last night, the Kamzhou-Beijing wheel received a telegram stating that it had encountered a strong wind in the waters off Mali Xi Ai Island in the North Pacific. The entire ship tilted and was flooded and about to sink. Currently, the crew and sailors have been rescued by a Kawasaki Company seagoing wheel. The crew and others are safe, but the ship is about to sink.

Land Value Tax to be Levied Soon 293

The collection of land value tax in this city has been prepared by the Financial and Land Bureaus since the beginning, and it has been a long time. Now I know that all the procedures for the collection have been arranged in order. However, the regulations on the collection, etc., were previously submitted to the Executive Yuan to temporarily order the Ministry of Interior and Finance to review them, but no reply has been received so far. In order to start the collection as soon as possible, the Municipal Government specifically telegraphed the Executive Yuan to order the Ministry of Interior and Finance to reply to the submitted regulations, etc., as soon as possible so that they can be announced and implemented. Therefore, the levying of land value tax is only waiting for the approval reply from the Executive Yuan, and the date should not be far away.

Case of Shooting Xi Lusheng 294

The Murderer Song A'er was Arrested

Xi Lusheng, a comprador of the former Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation and a native of Dongting Mountain, suddenly encountered a number of kidnappers on Fuzhou Road on December 6, 1929, intending to kidnap Xi and extort a huge sum of money. Xi resisted, causing him to be shot and injured by the bandits, and he died soon after. Subsequently, the police arrested one of the kidnappers, Shi Jinde, and handed him over to the First Special Court, which sentenced him to death. When Shi was interrogated, he confessed that Song A'er (ie Song Jiahua) from Tongzhou was the principal offender. At that time, Xi was shot and killed by Song. The police immediately searched for Song, but never found him. Until 10:10 AM yesterday morning, Chief Inspector of the General Patrol Room Pang Ruiqing and Shen Jinwen discovered that Song was hiding at No. 2, Lane 257, Caishi Road, French Concession, so they cooperated with detectives from the French Concession Police to go to the address and arrest Song, taking him back to the police station for detention. This morning, he was escorted to the Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu explained the previous situation, and said that the police investigation procedures were not yet complete, so they had not formally prosecuted and requested permission to detain him. Song also hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend him. Feng Shide, the head of the Criminal Division, verified the report, approved the police request, and ordered Song to be detained and questioned again at a later date.

Three Fires This Morning 295

Taopeng Road In a lane on Taopeng Road, Yangshupu, the Zhu Senhe Guanquan shop at No. 3, caught fire due to carelessness at around 8:00 AM this morning, and suddenly the roof was pierced, and the flames soared, and also affected the houses at No. 1 and No. 5 on the left and right. Later, the fire brigade drove a pump car to rush to rescue, and it was extinguished after a while. It is estimated that three houses were burned. The fire starter was arrested by the patrol and taken to the police station for verification.

Robison Road The Tonghe Nanhua store at No. 1209 to No. 1210, Yinhua Lane, Robison Road, West Shanghai, suddenly reported a fire at around 9:20 this morning, which was out of control. In a moment, three houses were turned into ashes. Fortunately, the fire brigade worked hard to put out the fire, and it did not affect the neighbors.

Xizang Road The Shanghai Zilaihuo Company at the intersection of Xizang Road and Xiamen Road touched the asphalt pool due to the strong wind, which caused it to burn. The machine parts were also on fire. After the fire brigade rushed to the scene after hearing the alarm, it was extinguished at around 4:00. Fortunately, the fire did not spread to the houses. It is estimated that about 1,000 yuan worth of asphalt was burned after the incident.

Commentary

A Consistent Offensive Strategy 296

— Ji'an

Our country's diplomacy has always been uncertain. Every time an incident occurs, we still use the simple prescription of treating the headache when the head hurts and treating the foot when the foot hurts to fight against the ferocious and terrifying disease demon, 丨丨nationalism, resulting in the entire modern diplomatic history being almost entirely bloody records of shrinking territory. Look! The beautiful Chinese-crabapple-leaf-style territory inherited from our ancestors for more than 4,000 years is already gradually becoming an incomplete mulberry leaf eaten by silkworms, with a corner missing yesterday and a piece missing today, isn't it?

The day before yesterday, a certain important person resolutely stated that the government's policy has always been consistent (how it was in the past), and will still be the same in the future. Then he said: Recently, a new diplomatic path has been negotiated, which is not only a softened compromise, but also an active and tough one. This fascinating diplomatic statement, which gives infinite hope, is like the sudden fragrance of roses to the countrymen, who feel refreshed and comforted in their hearts 丨

However, since the outbreak of the September 18th Incident, some have sought a battle with the Japanese army's iron hooves, while others have endured humiliation and sought peace, and still others have maintained an ambiguous attitude, hoping to maintain a situation of neither war nor peace for a long time. I wonder what exactly the consistent policy referred to by a certain important person refers to? But if the phrase "(how it was in the past, will still be the same in the future)" is reversed, it becomes "(if you want to know what the future will be like, just look at how it was in the past)." So, what exactly was the past like? The facts are clear, and we can (understand each other without speaking) 丨

(If you can't plant seedlings, you can't see the dike). The so-called consistent continental policy of the Japanese, the change of emperors, is like this, and the old overturned and new groups of cabinets are also like this. The Qing-Japanese War of 1894 was the beginning of its continental policy, the Russo-Japanese War of 1904, and the attack on Shenyang and the occupation of the Northeast on September 18, and even the recent capture of Rehe, all without exception are for its continental policy. People's consistent policy towards me is so grand and true, while my consistent policy towards people is so timid and false. Under the law of (when they extend, we contract, and when they contract, we extend), we can infer that the consistent policy in the mouth of our diplomats seems to be consistent) is indeed true, but the so-called (tough, active, new path) still needs to be resolved in the next episode in fact)

Ghost 298

— Ping

Since my wife returned to her mother's house the day before yesterday, only I am left in these old houses. During the day, I can open the front window and hear the laughter of the neighbors, relieving my loneliness. But when the darkness of night enveloped the earth, the lonely scene of the hometown made me think of ghosts and monsters. Unfortunately, I also caught a cold, lying drowsily on the bed, feeling uneasy in my heart. The courtyard was quiet in front and behind, and the occasional barking of dogs from the fields added to the terror of the night. I tossed and turned, unable to sleep, staring at the kerosene lamp on the table. The lamp wick shrank even smaller, and the sound of the watchman's gong came from the street in the distance.

Suddenly, there was a rustling movement in the patio, disturbing the grass leaves in the north ridge. The sound slowly moved and stopped at the corner of the house, as if it had struck the iron drainpipe. The ghost flashed across my eyes like lightning, and the hideous shadows flickered on the walls of the room. I covered myself with the quilt, and it seemed as if someone was pressing down on me, and beads of sweat broke out all over my body. My hands and feet could no longer move on their own. Suddenly, with a (thump), as if something heavy had fallen into the water. I tried to stick my head out and brighten the lamp wick, thinking of getting up to find out what was going on, but in the end (ghost), I didn't dare to look out into the patio.

Because I thought of ghosts, the ghost stories I had heard as a child all came to mind, as if there were ghosts moving around my bedroom. In the silence of terror, I don't know how long it took before I fell asleep.

When I woke up the next day, I was still lying in bed very tired when I heard the maid's surprised cry.

(The kitten drowned in the water tank!)

That was a beloved kitten of mine, which I had only taken in a week ago. It slept in my room every night. Since I had been sick for two days, I had thrown the kitten out of my memory. Last night, I was able to think carefully about the origin of this sound and made a night of self-disturbance with doubts about ghosts. I put on my clothes and walked out. The maid carried the stiff-legged kitten in from

outside, as if to say (it's dead). I looked at it apologetically, if I had been brave enough to get up last night, wouldn't I have been able to save it? Ghosts, suspecting ghosts, lightly sent off a small life.

I also thought that the defeat in Shenyang and the loss of Rehe were not caused by the terror of ghosts like last night? Although the kitten cannot catch mice for the time being, it is a cat itself, so at least there is hope of catching mice. I lightly sacrificed a small life, and my heart was as if it had been cut.

Shop Assistant Communication

Such Parents 300

— Jiang Shi-mei Ying

Mr. Editor,

I have been married for six years, and my husband treats me very well. For the first four years, our situation was just barely sustainable. Since last summer, my husband's business has become very successful; therefore, last winter, we moved into a Western-style house with rent of one hundred several tens of taels, and at the same time bought a new-style automobile. By right, my life should be happy and comfortable; but I have my own worries. My parents' family is in a difficult situation; I have eight siblings in total, apart from my two older sisters and me, who are already married, there are still three younger brothers and two younger sisters, who are still studying in school. My parents are really unable to support them. Furthermore, my two older sisters are married to ordinary men, so logically I should subsidize my parents' household expenses or help with my younger siblings' tuition fees. However, my parents are people who bully the kind and fear the wicked, and are extremely snobbish. So, before my husband prospered, they bullied me greatly, and also treated my husband badly. Now, because they want me to subsidize them, they have completely changed their attitude and treat me very attentively. They often ask to borrow my car, and beg me with tears and pleas to subsidize them with a hundred yuan per month for household expenses. I am unwilling to use the money my husband earned with his sweat and blood to subsidize such a snobbish family; but I cannot bear their tearful and pleading behavior. Please answer me, I am waiting under this difficult problem! With respect,

Yours Sincerely, Jiang Shi-mei Ying

Editor's Note: Human emotions are snobbish; this has been the case since ancient times. In the past, when Su Qin was still unsuccessful, he was also (treated such that his wife did not weave, his sister-in-law did not cook, and his parents did not speak to him). Later, when he wore the seals of office of six states and was about to persuade the King of Chu, when he passed through Luoyang, his parents greeted him in the suburbs thirty li away, his wife looked at him askance and listened attentively, and his sister-in-law crawled on her belly, bowed four times, and knelt down to thank him. However, we have never heard it said that Su Qin, because his parents, older brother, sister-in-law, and wife treated him badly when he was unsuccessful, therefore took revenge on them. Mrs. Jiang and Mr. Jiang, even if you suffered some grievances in the past, now that you have prospered and they are seeking your help, their insincere compliance is sufficient punishment for them. You should remember the bond of kinship and not hold it in your heart, seeking retribution! If your husband, because he is after all still a step removed, remembers the past and is unwilling to care for them, you must still persuade him from the side. How can you adopt a policy of (requiting every grievance) between parents, older brothers, and older sisters!

Novel

Fleeting Time in a Dream (8th installment) 301

— Qin Shouou

Among them were complimentary tickets for (Wanli Hong), (Qin Lou), (Fragrant Concubine), etc., meal tickets resembling paper money, powder paper for women, and bills from hotels and restaurants; the most shocking, however, were several pawn tickets, indispensable to every fallen person. The only souvenirs after pursuing pleasure and waking from a beautiful dream.

(Humph!) Mother was so angry that her face turned white. That night, she cried all night long. Wu Yi couldn't help but think of his grandfather and what he had said when he was dying, and he felt very sad. Starting the next day, he actually became a law-abiding citizen for a week.

A week later, the women's phone calls and the urging of his friends gradually disturbed his restless heart again. However, in order to avoid upsetting his mother, he decided to change his public actions into secret actions. Every night, after one o'clock, he would return home on time as usual without making a sound, deliberately making some noise to let his mother know that he had returned. Fortunately, he was lying in the attic. After pretending to sleep in bed for a while, he quietly sneaked downstairs and out the door. However, when going downstairs, he had to take off his leather shoes first, tiptoe, and slowly inch his way down the stairs. When he returned at dawn, he did the same thing.

He lived such a secretive and degenerate inhuman life for more than a year. One night, he slipped out as usual to spend his sweet spring night leaning on red and green, and only returned at 7:30 in the morning. Sleepy-eyed, he pushed open the door of the attic, breathed a sigh of relief, and was about to take off his clothes when suddenly he felt something more in front of him.

Under the fish-belly white dawn light shining in from the window, an old lady with a pale face and straight eyes was vaguely visible, collapsed on the deep red floor, with one hand still firmly gripping a jewelry store invoice for one hundred and twenty yuan.

Wu Yi trembled all over as if he had been electrocuted. He had realized, he had awakened: but his poor mother would never stand up again ㈥ Three Friends

"Little Wu, what are you still afraid of now? Tonight at the 'Mingzhu'!" Less than a month after Wu Yi's mother died, a group of degenerate friends who didn't want to be born on the same day but wished to die on the same day came to his door one by one, grinning and urging him to continue doing the work of "degeneration not yet successful, comrades still need to work hard." In their eyes, Wu Yi's mother's death was truly a great happy event for Wu Yi, and they almost congratulated him.

However, Wu Yi had completely awakened. He knew that from now on, no one could protect him anymore, and future success or failure depended on his every action. Therefore, he brazenly turned his face, cursed these worthless friends, and chased them away with a barrage of blows, staying alone at home for forty-nine days.

This day was the first day he returned to work at the Star Daily after suffering a great enemy. For some unknown reason, as soon as he walked into the newsroom, he felt a burning sensation on his face, as if he had a terrible case of hypocrisy, and he was so ashamed that he didn't even have the courage to greet his colleagues.

He hung his head and sat awkwardly at his desk. Looking at the desk, there was already a high stack of letters: looking at them one by one, a large portion were invitations to drink flower wine and invitations to gambling dens. There were also a few letters from friends asking him to publish publicity messages, among which there was only one letter expressing condolences to him.

This was written by his old classmate Wang Yulin. Wang Yulin's entry into history was not very glorious either, but he was not one of the people who contributed to Wu Yi's degeneration, because after graduating from the Education Department of X University, he went to Japan to study law, and after graduating two years later, he was busy opening a law firm, so he had not been in contact with Wu Yi for a long time. This letter was something that Wu Yi could not have anticipated, especially the sincerity of the words in his letter, which greatly moved Wu Yi.

"I've decided to see him tomorrow!" After reading many letters, Wu Yi hung his head and muttered silently to himself.

"Are you Mr. Wu Yi! I've admired you for a long time! I've admired you for a long time!" At some point, a new colleague had been added to the seat opposite Wu Yi. A young man with a dark complexion, a strong build, and wearing a pair of large Locke glasses. This person didn't wait for Wu Yi to greet him, but put on a smile and started to be perfunctory. "My brother is Zhao Qianli. I studied psychology at the University of Pennsylvania in the United States. Recently, I returned to China and was found by Mr. Zhang XX here to serve as the editor of international telecommunications. In the future, I will often have to ask Mr. Wu for advice!"

A friend who had been eating flour-flag bread for many years could be so humble; Wu Yi couldn't help but feel a sense of goodwill towards Zhao Qianli. So the two of them opened up and talked as if they were old friends meeting again; somehow, their conversation suddenly shifted to the issue of making friends.

"In modern times, friends have become interest exchange devices." Zhao Qianli said with the cold and witty expression that every psychologist often has, as if lecturing: "If you don't have money or power, you can forget about making friends for the rest of your life; or there may be someone who is willing to condescend to you, then either there are some antiques in your family worth his affection, or [illegible character] thief, or you must have a beautiful wife!"

Film Special

Anecdotes of the Mouse Cartoonist, Walt Disney 302

— Jing Ruo

I think people who often watch movies have seen the mouse cartoons that are often shown before the feature film, right? These films are very lively, humorous, and interesting. Walt Disney, the creator of these cartoons, seems to have been introduced in this magazine before. I will now describe a few of his anecdotes, which I think will also be welcome to the readers who love to watch his films, right? He originally worked for an oil company, but because he seemed very interested in satirical and humorous drawings, he often made paintings for recreation. He first made a satirical cartoon film for the Kasaas movie theater, and later made several satirical fairy tale films in a row to be shown in churches and schools, but he was not successful. At this time, he only had a pair of pants, a flannel coat, and a film camera. But he was not discouraged. He sold the camera for forty dollars and ran to Hollywood. His brother was a vendor in Hollywood. Without asking the reason, he took the two hundred and fifty dollars his brother had saved as capital and engaged in painting again. This time it was finally successful, and his interest was immediately recognized by people.

When he was making films for Universal Pictures, the people in the company thought he was too extravagant and suddenly canceled his contract. At this time, he happened to be in New York. He couldn't bear to let his twenty assistants lose their jobs. He immediately organized a Walt Disney Film Company.

He is now considered a great success. However, the reason why he is so diligently engaged in this business is not to get rich, but only for interest. Once. A friend asked him how it feels to be rich. He only replied (I don't know, I didn't pay attention to these). This is true, he didn't lie. He still lives in the old English-style house he lived in ten years ago.

But his success is not accidental, he really has talent. He was very interested in animals and painting when he was a child: he started painting at the age of five. He used thick asphalt as ink and the white wall as paper. All the books in his house were painted with many fraudulent pictures.

He still often goes to the zoo to take animal films as the only entertainment during his holidays. His wife often complains that she is a mouse widow.

He is very generous to the people he employs. He always tries to make their lives comfortable, he prepares all kinds of facilities for them. He lets them take generous salaries and only do a few things. I think such an employer is rare, and only people like him who do not aim to make money can do it.

Film Review

Review of Considerate Handling With Care 303

— Ling He

The structure is good, but the meaning is non-existent.

The director's skills are skilled, Nanjing screening

Here is a rather tortuous story.

A female clerk named Helen works in a department store and takes care of her sister's two children. One child is arrested for stealing milk to feed a cat. During the hearing, a young lawyer learns that he is Helen's nephew. Helen is the lawyer's former lover, so the two lovers are able to meet again. Later, the lawyer punishes the two children because of the evil cat, but Helen loves them as if they were her own, and the two eventually break up. In the end, the lawyer is robbed while dealing with a lawsuit and is rescued by the two children, so the two lovers are able to reunite and love the two children.

In such a story, the screenwriter has used some ideas very well. He has interwoven the entire plot quite tightly, without any coercion. Although there are many jokes, they are not so stiff as to make people bored. The best thing is that he mobilized hundreds of children, which is a new aspect in Hollywood films. But why did he write such a script? What is the intention? This is something we can't figure out. So this film has no meaning at all, it's just that he conceived such a script in his mind.

However, the director's use of this film is very flexible and skillful. He simplifies the unnecessary key points as much as possible, so that the audience can have a clear understanding of the progress of the whole play in front of short shots. He paid special attention to the performances of the two children. Buster Phelps, who is less than ten years old, is able to give such a valuable performance under his command, which of course is due to him. At the same time, he can always show his cleverness in the important key points: for example, when a child escapes out of the window, causing the washbasin to fall and make a crashing sound, when the robber hears the sound and enters, the two children improvise and play tricks on the robber. This is also a joke, but it is very clever. As for the police coming to arrest the robber, it is also very natural, but this is also the strictness of the screenwriter.

In terms of performance, although James Dunn and JBooots Mallors are the main characters in this play, the performance is very mediocre and the tasks they undertake are not seen as important. As for that child, Phipps D. Fils, he is very good. He is so realistic and lively that the protagonist cannot help but be overshadowed by it.

Lighting, scenery, and sound are not characteristic, but the editing is still ingenious.

Overall, this is not a very good film, but it is still worth watching.

The Education Bureau Forbids the Filming of Humiliating Films 304

The Da Zhonghua Film Company on Xieshang Road in this city was opened by a Westerner, Bailideng. It has now been found by the Nanjing Film Inspection Committee that the company has secretly filmed many humiliating films. The Ministry of Education and Internal Affairs has been requested to transfer this to the local authorities of this city for thorough investigation. It is now known that the Education Bureau has sent personnel to investigate. According to reports, the company has been reorganized into the Dahua Company, and its business has been suspended, but the address has been rented to the Qianghua Film Company, which does have [illegible characters] films, so the Education Bureau has ordered the company to stop filming on [illegible characters] days. The Municipal Film Review Committee and the Public Security Bureau will assist in stopping it.

Habitual Expressions on the Silver Screen 305

— Hua Ming

After watching many movies, before watching a certain movie, you don't need to know who the characters in the play are. If [illegible characters] wears broken leather shoes and walks with a figure-eight step, wears a narrow-brimmed black hat, you can tell at a glance that it is Chaplin. A thin man and a fat man making jokes together must be Laurel and Hardy. A hand often stroking the hair must be Bibi Danier. Wearing a skirt like an unfolded folding fan and constantly looking back at the clothes must be Jane Gaynor. It is more accurate than recognizing faces and will never be mistaken. On the silver screen, each actor has their own habitual expressions, which we can remember in detail. The success of these expressions is roughly divided into two reasons. The first is because they are deliberately made and become a habit, like Chaplin, Laurel, and Hardy. The second is a natural habit, like Bibi Danier and Jane Gaynor. Now, let's roughly record the habitual movements of each actor:

Mary Trance shakes like a rain-drenched chicken; Mary Pickford's curly and very long golden hair; Joan Crawford walks very fast with big steps; Li Lingkan stares straight ahead; Clara Bao drags her messy hair and stomps her feet; Ann Harding pulls her clothes from time to time when walking; Keen Harlow walks with her hips protruding, turns her head back from her shoulders, pretending to smile, and Greta Garbo raises her head and looks down.

Among the male actors, Clark Gable smiles a lot, Fan Pengke raises his hand to show courage, and Li Que Dikes flexes his muscles and clenches his teeth to pretend to be fearless, Wallace Piley sneers and scratches his ears, Tommy Hicks speaks in the ear of his horse Tommy, Li Que Baisames clenches his teeth to show fierceness, Li Ang Barimur shakes his head and ears like a fierce bear locked in a cage, John Barimur stands upright and arrogantly; Louis Stone bends over and is good at flattering, Adolf Meng Yu smiles with his eyebrows and eyes; Peis Kaiden is coldly aggressive; Lei Men Nuo Vallo looks at women without looking at others; Yare Qiao Ersheng dances with his feet off the ground; Locke widens his eyes from his glasses and pretends to be frightened, and Xifolai wears his straw hat crookedly. Many habitual movements can arouse interest, such as Chaplin, Peis Kaiden, etc., but only limited to comedians, as for other roles, they are annoying. So several actors like Helen Hayes, Naoma Shila, etc. have all removed their habitual movements, so they can't be found.

Metropolis Morning-Prelude 306

— Guo Shenghong

Another film that shouts for the masses and closely follows the times is Lianhua's new film, Metropolis Morning.

Ms. Wang Renmei plays a simple and lively village girl in (Metropolis Morning), innocent, romantic, lively and lovely. Gao Zhanfei plays a poor illegitimate child, and his brave and strong physique is just right for the coolie he plays who is struggling in a painful life. When he plays the scene where he understands his life experience on a stormy night and rushes straight to his biological father's house like a crazy evil spirit, the audience's heartstrings are tense and shaken with the character's mind.

The plot of this film is very tortuous, compact and moving, and there is no dull place from beginning to end. The young director Cai Chusheng also has a history in the directing world. His direction of (Metropolis Morning) may not disappoint.

Re-introducing (Pursuit) 307

— Pei Yuan

Love is originally pure and sacred, it is indomitable in the face of power and wealth, but in today's society, women who generally like vanity only know that the price of love is money. Therefore, storms often arise in the sea of love, and there is no good result in the end.

The (Pursuit) recently produced by Tianyi Company is aimed at the love problems of young men and women today. Its central consciousness is to depict the vanity of modern women and make powerful criticisms, to write sacred and pure love, to serve as a lesson for men and women, and at the same time to advance to us; a warning of (the sea of love is vast, and the end is the shore)

Another point worth mentioning is that several of the grand scenes in (Pursuit) are indeed worthy of the four-character commentary (magnificent and luxurious). At the same time, in terms of lighting and photography, there is much progress compared to (Double Mandarin Ducks in a Sea of Sin).

Marlene initially protested, but now suddenly sent her lawyer Robb Leun to discuss with the company's lawyer, and the result was satisfactory, and the film can continue.

Movie novel

Red Dust (3) 309

— Jack

(Adding one more is also fine! But Dennis sneered and left the room with Mike.

After the sound of his heavy footsteps faded along the balcony, Dan sprang up from the bed. She grabbed Jude's arm and dragged him out to the balcony. Then, she returned to the room, slammed the door shut, climbed onto the bed, and fell asleep.

But Dennis and Mike returned to the living room and sat down to eat. Mike reached for his bowl and filled it with green beans, but Dennis poured himself a glass of brandy and drank it down. Mike then urged him to eat something. They exchanged a few words, but Dennis poured another glass of wine. They continued to talk.

"Do you think I'll grow old here?" Dennis said.

"Why don't you take a trip to Saigon?" Mike replied, his mouth full of beans, while scrutinizing him closely.

"There's no one trustworthy here, how can I go to Saigon?" Dennis drank another glass of wine.

"Actually!" Mike said with a teasing tone, "It wouldn't be difficult to come from Saigon:"

"Humph!" Dennis said sadly. He leaned back in his chair, half-closed his eyes, and smiled wistfully. "Mike, once in London after the war, there was a girl like cream-colored velvet—" His face tightened, and he stopped speaking.

After dinner, Dennis unfolded a farm map and listlessly examined it, instructing Mike on the work plan for tomorrow.

Outside, a tiger roared, as if challenging the night. Mike stood up and walked to the balcony.

"Jude is lying across the balcony," Mike reported.

"Let him lie there."

"Alright, I'm going to sleep. See you tomorrow, Dennis."

"See you tomorrow, Mike." Dennis opened his typewriter and inserted a sheet of paper. He was busy typing when suddenly a light sound arose beside him, distracting him.

Dan tiptoed into the room, sat on the table, and looked at the stern, nonchalant face with great interest. (To be continued)
